triggers {
  name: "Exit"
  events {
    ops {
      functionName: "On Item Interaction"
      args {
        call_value {
          functionName: "Get Map Item (InteractableObject)"
          args {
            string_value: "528417243363316011007e8c"
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }
  conditions {
  }
  actions {
    ops {
      functionName: "Open Scene"
      args {
        call_value {
          functionName: "Get Map Item (Scene)"
          args {
            string_value: "the puyullup barrens"
          }
        }
      }
    }
    ops {
      functionName: "Set Variable (int)"
      args {
        call_value {
          functionName: "Get Story Variable (int)"
          args {
            string_value: "51f15c62336331d02c00440e"
          }
          args {
            string_value: "Travel"
          }
        }
      }
      args {
        int_value: 5
      }
    }
  }
  isActive: true
  idRef {
    id: "528416f53363316011007e8a"
  }
  elseActions {
  }
  is_oneshot: true
}
triggers {
  name: "Fade"
  events {
    ops {
      functionName: "Get Map Item (Event)"
      args {
        string_value: "Fade Out / In"
      }
    }
  }
  conditions {
  }
  actions {
    ops {
      functionName: "Fade Camera Out"
      args {
        float_value: 1
      }
      args {
        float_value: 0
      }
    }
    ops {
      functionName: "Fade Camera In"
      args {
        float_value: 1
      }
      args {
        float_value: 1
      }
    }
  }
  isActive: true
  idRef {
    id: "529054db3363317828005b3a"
  }
  elseActions {
  }
  is_oneshot: false
}
triggers {
  name: "Variable Fade"
  events {
    ops {
      functionName: "Get Map Item (Event)"
      args {
        string_value: "Variable Fade"
      }
    }
  }
  conditions {
    ops {
      functionName: "Comparison (int)"
      args {
        call_value {
          functionName: "Get Story Variable (int)"
          args {
            string_value: "51f15c62336331d02c00440e"
          }
          args {
            string_value: "FadeVariable"
          }
        }
      }
      args {
        call_value {
          functionName: "Get Preset Value (int)"
          args {
            string_value: "Comparison Ops"
          }
          args {
            int_value: 4
          }
        }
      }
      args {
        int_value: 15
      }
    }
  }
  actions {
    ops {
      functionName: "Fade Camera Out"
      args {
        float_value: 0
      }
      args {
        float_value: 0
      }
    }
    ops {
      functionName: "Fade Camera In"
      args {
        float_value: 1
      }
      args {
        call_value {
          functionName: "Arithmetic (float)"
          args {
            float_value: 15
          }
          args {
            call_value {
              functionName: "Get Preset Value (int)"
              args {
                string_value: "Arithmetic Ops"
              }
              args {
                int_value: 1
              }
            }
          }
          args {
            call_value {
              functionName: "Convert (int) to (float)"
              args {
                call_value {
                  functionName: "Get Story Variable (int)"
                  args {
                    string_value: "51f15c62336331d02c00440e"
                  }
                  args {
                    string_value: "FadeVariable"
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }
  isActive: true
  idRef {
    id: "52904fa33363317828005ba7"
  }
  elseActions {
    ops {
      functionName: "Fade Camera Out"
      args {
        float_value: 0
      }
      args {
        float_value: 0
      }
    }
    ops {
      functionName: "Fade Camera In"
      args {
        float_value: 1
      }
      args {
        float_value: 1
      }
    }
  }
  is_oneshot: false
}
